 vah is gathjod ke zarie sabit kar rahi thi ki bijepi jammu-kashmir tak main shashan kar rahi he jo lagbhag naammumkin mana jaataa tha
 In fact, Kashmir has been just a geography for the BJP, which it has been describing as an integral part of India
 jis kashmiriat kii baat pichley dinon rajnath singh ne kii, uske prati bijepi main jaraa bhi samvedansheeltaa hoti to is behad najuk mode par vah sarkaar giraane kaa kaam nahin karti
 But Kashmir is a political issue for him which is useful in Bihar and UP elections
 anuchhed 370 (jise bijepi dhara 370 bataaya karti he) kii samaj ho yaa na ho, lekin ise hataane kii maang bijepi kaaryakartaaon kii baari lokapriy maang he
 Actually, this decision of 2018 is the beginning of 2019 preparations for BJP
 2019 main bijepi jis hindutv ke agenda ko aage badhanaa chaahati he, uski raah main ek roda kashmir bhi tha or mahabuuba se uski dosti bhi thi
 Whenever moving forward on this agenda, she would talk about mismatched alliances of Karnataka or UP, the question of alliances with PDP would be put in front of her
 vah sarkaar main shaamil rahete na kathua ke aropiyon kaa saath de sakati thi or na hi anuchhed 370 hataane kii maang kar sakati thi
 On the contrary, if Mehbooba had remained adamant on her policies, it would have been necessary for the BJP to take a soft stance on Kashmir, after which it would also face criticism within its allied organizations
 bijepi kii samarthan vaapasi se mahabuuba ne bhi shaayad raahat kii saans lee jo lagaataar yah mahasoos kar rahi thi ki bijepi ke saath se uskaa dam ghut rahaa he
 So now in 2019, BJP will again raise the tone of Kashmir
 goraksha, lav jehad, teen talaak or aatankwaad ke alaava kashmir vah chauthaa mudda hoga jis par bijepi vot maangegi
 But who will worry about Kashmir? Only the liberal elements of Kashmir will have to do this
 kashmir kaa raajnneetik hal ek sawaal he, uski saamaajikta behaal karnaa kahin zyaada badi chunauti ban gaya he
 The comments aaj kashmir dard se anthti ek deh kaa naam he
 There is a palpable feeling of steplessness within him
 uskaa ilaaj sena kii surgery nahin he, iskaa ilaaj bharose kaa malaham he
 The cease-fire with which the last disagreement remained within the Mehbooba government, could be met with that ointment
 durbhaagya se jo log yah malaham chin rahe hai, vahi bharat kii aam taur par anushaasit maani jane vaali sena ko bhi kashmir main khalanaayak banane ko majaboor kar rahe hai- aakhir kisi bhi samaaj main sena kii dirghakaalin maujuudagi dar, ub or antat nafrat hi paidaa kar sakati he
 Then when the army goes into such a difficult area, then it is very possible that not only terrorists but some common people will come in the grip of its action and eventually it will spoil the atmosphere as usual
 lekin kashmir main aman or malaham kaa sawaal sirf kashmir kaa nahin, us puure bharat kaa sawaal he jo loktantric chetana or maanviya garima main bharosa karata he
 If Kashmir does not survive with its natural humanity, it will soon have an impact on the rest of India as well
 hinsa ko asardaar hathiyaar maanane vaali sattayen duusare ilaaqon main bhi iske prayog se hichakengi nahin
 Therefore, the battle of Aman in Kashmir is the battle of the whole of India
 ise shabdadambaron se aage jaakar ladanaa hoga

 Clearly, the picture has become more frightening over the years
 ab kashmir main sawaal maanavadhikaar hanan yaa aatankwaad ke khatme kaa nahin he, vahaan chunauti kashmir ko ek lagaataar chal rahe yuddh kii maansikta se baahar nikaalane kii he, vahaan lagaataar mushkil ho rahe loktantr ko nae sire se behaal karne kii he
 Forgetting this challenge, the BJP decided to break away from the state government and implement Governor's rule there
 is faisle ke peeche usne jitani sari vajahen bataayin, ve sab 2014 main bhi maujuud thim, jab bijepi-pidipi ne milakar sarkaar banaai thi
 The trenches of mistrust were still as deep as they are today
 lekin tab bijepi ko apni rashtriya pahunch kaa dayera badhanaa tha
 Through this alliance, she was proving that the BJP was ruling in Jammu and Kashmir, which was considered impossible
 darasal kashmir bijepi ke liye mahaj ek bhugol rahaa he jise vah bharat kaa akhand hissaa bataati rahi he
 If the BJP had a little sensitivity towards the Kashmiriyat that Rajnath Singh had talked about in the past, then at this very delicate point, he would not work to topple the government
 lekin kashmir uske liye ek raajnneetik mudda he jo bihar or upi ke chunaavon main kaam aata he
 Whether or not Article 370 (which BJP describes as Section 370) is understood, the demand for its removal is a huge popular demand of BJP workers
 darasal 2018 kaa yah faisalaa bijepi ke liye 2019 kii taiyaari kii shuruyaat he
 The Hindutva agenda that the BJP wants to pursue in 2019, Kashmir had a hurdle in its path and its friendship with Mehbooba
 jab bhi is agenda par aage badhate hue vah karnataka yaa upi ke bemail gathjod kii baat karti, uske saamne pidipi ke saath gathjod kaa sawaal rakh diya jaataa
 She could neither support the accused of Kathua nor demand removal of Article 370 while joining the government
 ulte agar mahabuuba apni nitiyon par adi rahati to bijepi ke liye kashmir par naram rukh baratna lajimi hota jiske baad phir vah apane sahyogi sanghathanon ke bheetar bhi aalochana jhelti
 Mehbooba may have also breathed a sigh of relief from the bjp's backing, which felt that she was choking along with the BJP
 to ab 2019 main bijepi phir se kashmir kaa raag chhedegi
 Apart from cow protection, love jihad, triple talaq and terrorism, Kashmir will be the fourth issue on which BJP will seek votes
 lekin kashmir kii phikr koun karegaa? yah kashmir ke udaaravaadi tatwon ko hi kerani padegi
 The political solution of Kashmir is a question, restoring its sociality has become a much bigger challenge
 tippaniyan Today, Kashmir is the name of a body that aches with pain
 uske bheetar sautelepan kaa ek chatpataata ehsaas he
 His treatment is not army surgery, its treatment is an ointment of faith
 jis sangharsh-viraam ko lekar aakiri asahmati mahabuuba sarkaar ke bheetar rahi, usee se vah malaham mil saktaa tha
 Unfortunately, the people who are snatching this ointment are forcing India's generally disciplined army to become villains in Kashmir - after all, the army's long-term presence in any society creates fear, boredom and ultimately hatred
 Can do
 phir sena jab aise mushkil ilaake main jaaegi to yah bahut sambhav he ki uski karrwai kii chapet main sirf aatankwaadi nahin, kuch aam log bhi aaenge or antat isse hameshaa kii tarah maahaul kharaab hoga
 But the question of peace and ointment in Kashmir is not only of Kashmir, but the question of the whole of India, who believes in democratic consciousness and human dignity
 kashmir agar apni sahaj maanviyata ke saath nahin bachegaa to der-saber baaki bharat par bhi iskaa asar padegaa
 The governments which consider violence as an effective weapon will not hesitate to use it in other areas also
 isliye kashmir main aman kii ladaai puure hindustan kii ladaai he

 philhal bacchee kii haalat sthir bataai ja rahi he

 kaamkaaji logon kaa zyaadaatar samay offis main bitta he
 In such a situation, if the atmosphere and the boss is not good then you can be a victim of depression
 iskaa asar na keval aapke kaamkaaj balki maansik sthiti par bhi padataa he
 There are a lot of problems in working with a boss who stops all the time
 naukari chhod denine paristhitiyon se nipatane kaa koi hal nahin he kyonki ho saktaa he ki duusare offis main bhi aapkaa saamana kuch aise hi bos se ho jaae
 However, there is no such problem in this world which does not have a solution
 bas jarurat kuch baton kaa khyal rakhane kii he
 You can deal with your boss with the help of these tips: 1
 agar aapkaa bos aapako kaaphi pareshaan kar rahaa he to sabase pehle yah jaanane kii koshish karen ki kahin aap offis politics kaa shikaar to nahin ho rahe hai
 Most of the problems in the office are due to this reason
 agar offis politics ke kaaran aisa ho rahaa he to apnebaas se jald se jald baat karenor unki galatfahami ko dur karen
 2
 offis aap kaam karne jate hai na ki kisi kii shikaayat karne or kamajori bataane ke liye
 Just be mean to your work in office
 apane sahakarmiyon ke saath acha vyavhaar banaae rakhen magar unase kaam kii hi baaten karen to zyada behatar hoga
 3
 agar bos sidhe aapako koi kamsonpta he to use jaldi se jaldi puraa karen
 Always try to do a better job on your behalf so that the boss does not get a chance to complain unnecessarily
 4
 If the boss is not listening to you, then write a mail and say your point
 kai baar aisa hota he ki bos ko lagata he ki aap galati bhi kar rahe hai or palatakar jawaab bhi de rahe hai
 Sending mail is an easy way to avoid this situation, because if any reply is received in an unprofessional manner, you will have a record of it
 5
 It is better to talk peacefully than to argue and show anger
 ho saktaa he ki gusse main baat karne se baat banane kii bajaay bighad jaae or uskaa khamiyaja aapako uthaanaa pade
 So speak your words but wisely and calmly
 6
 If something has gone wrong that is difficult for you to handle, then you can take help of your colleagues
 sahyogiyon ke alaava aap yah dekhen ki offis main bos kaa kareebi koun he, unhen apni baat samajhane kii koshish karen or apni sthiti ko bataaen

 The case of murder of a Dalit person has come to light once again in Gujarat
 yahaan ranpur-barwaala sadak se guzar rahe dalit sarpanch ke pati ko 6 logon ne peet-peet kar maar daalaa
 This matter is only on Wednesday
 51 saal ke manjibhai solanki ko logon ne itnaa maaraa kii vah buree tarah ghayal ho gaya, jiske baad manjibhai ne kisi ko phone kar ye soochna di lekin baad main unhone dam tod diya
 On the phone, Manjibhai told that his motorcycle was hit by a car, after that 5-6 people came and beat him
 logon ne unhen lathi-dandon se maaraa
 Manjibhai is the husband of Geeta Solanki, sarpanch of Jalia village in Ranpur taluka
 jab solanki ko ahmedabad ke civil aspataal main le jaaya gaya, to doctoron ne use mrit ghoshit kiya
 a video of this incident is also going viral on social media, in which Manjibhai Solanki is lying injured on the road
 or unke rishtedaar unhen aspataal le jane kii koshish kar rahe hai
 In this video, he himself is saying, 'while he was going on a motorcycle, a car hit him
 baad main 5-6 logon ne unhen lathi-dandon se peeta
 'let me tell you that last year Manjibhai Solanki and his wife demanded protection from the police

 isse pehle 2013-14 main bhi pisibi ke chairman rahe sethi ne adhyaksh chunane ke liye board ke sadasyon kaa aabhaar vyakt kiya

 After becoming the chairman, Najam Sethi also made a big statement on india-pakistan cricket relations
 unhone kaha ki wo bharat ke saath dwipaksheeya siries ke liye koi darwaja band nahin karne vaale hai

 ’aapako bataa den pisibi ke pichley adhyaksh shehryaar khan ne bayaan diya tha ki unke kaarykaal kii sabase badi naakaami bharat or pakistan ke cricket rishton ko behaal nahin kar paanaa tha
